    city_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    city_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    population INT
);


CREATE TABLE sensors (
    sensor_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    sensor_type VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);


CREATE TABLE events (
    event_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    event_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    event_date DATE,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);


CREATE TABLE weather (
    weather_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    temperature INT,
    humidity FLOAT,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);
</t><stat>INSERT INTO city (city_id, city_name, population) VALUES (1, 'New York City', 8623000);</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE city (
    city_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    city_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    population INT
);


CREATE TABLE sensors (
    sensor_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    sensor_type VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);


CREATE TABLE events (
    event_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    event_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    event_date DATE,
    city_id INT,

    sensor_type VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,

    city_id INT,
